    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
      var confirmButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.idverify-section__info--confirm--button');
      var profileCheckAreas = document.querySelectorAll('.mypage-check-area');

      confirmButtons.forEach(function (confirmButton) {
        confirmButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
          profileCheckAreas.forEach(function (area) {
            area.style.display = 'none';
          });

          localStorage.setItem('mypage-check-close', true);
        });
      });

      // ローカルストレージの値をチェックして、非表示状態にする
      if (localStorage.getItem('mypage-check-close')) {
        profileCheckAreas.forEach(function (profileCheckArea) {
          profileCheckArea.style.display = 'none';
        });
      }
    });

    function gtmClickBadge(badge_status, page_type) {
      dataLayer = dataLayer || [];
      let event_label = '';

      if (page_type === 'drawer') {
        event_label = 'click_drawer_identification_badge';
      } else if (page_type === 'mypage') {
        event_label = 'click_mypage_identification_badge';
      }

      dataLayer.push({
        event: 'fireEvent',
        eventData: {
          event_name: '',
          event_parameter: {
            view: 0,
            event_label: event_label,
            click_label: badge_status,
          },
        },
      });
    }
  </script>

  <script>
    function gaSaleOnlyCheck() {
      dataLayer = dataLayer || []
      if ( !document.getElementById("selling-box").checked ) {
        if (true) {
          ga('send', 'event', 'ui_action', 'search', 'click_search_sale_only');
          dataLayerPush('click_search_sale_only');
        } else if (false) {
          ga('send', 'event', 'ui_action', 'search', 'click_brand_sale_only');
          dataLayerPush('click_brand_sale_only');
        }
      }
    }

    function dataLayerPush(label) {
      dataLayer.push({
        event:"fireEvent",
        eventData:{
          event_name:"",
          event_parameter:{
            view:0,
            event_label: label,
          }
        }
      });
    }
  </script>

<script>
  function gaTrackOrder(order) {
    dataLayer = dataLayer || []
    var pathArray = location.pathname.split('/');
    var gaLabel = '';
    var dimension3 = '';
    switch (pathArray[1]) {
      case 'category':
        gaLabel = 'select_category_order'
        break;
      case 'brand':
        gaLabel = 'click_brand_order'
        break;
      case 'search':
        gaLabel = 'click_search_order'
        break;
    }
    switch (order) {
      case'おすすめ順':
        dimension3 = 'recommend';
        break;
      case'新着順':
        dimension3 = 'new';
        break;
      case'いいねが多い順':
        dimension3 = 'like';
        break;
      case'安い順':
        dimension3 = 'cheap';
        break;
      case'高い順':
        dimension3 = 'expansive';
        break;
    }
    ga('send', 'event', 'ui_action', 'search', gaLabel, { 'dimension3': dimension3 });
    dataLayer.push({
      event:"fireEvent",
      eventData:{
        event_name:"",
        event_parameter:{
          view:0,
          event_label: gaLabel,
          search_type: dimension3
        }
      }
    });
  }
</script>

                </div>
              </div>

  function gaLikeClick(){

    var dimension3 = '';

      case 'category':

    });
  }

  function gaLikeClick(){
    var pathArray = location.pathname.split('/');
    var dimension3 = '';
    switch(pathArray[1]) {
      case 'category':
        dimension3 = 'category';
        break;
      case 'brand':
        dimension3 = 'brand';
        break;
      case 'shop':
        dimension3 = 'shop';
        break;
      case 'search':
        dimension3 = 'search';
        break;
    }
    ga('send', 'event', 'ui_action', 'search', 'click_like', { 'dimension3': dimension3,
    });
  }

        dimension3 = 'category';

        dimension3 = 'search';

    });
  }

<script>
  const user_w_size = window.innerWidth;
  let targetElement = null;
  let isTargetVisible = false;

  window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    let parentElements;
    let childElement = null;

    if (user_w_size < 980) {
      parentElements = document.querySelectorAll('.related-keywords__sp');
    } else {
      parentElements = document.querySelectorAll('.related-keywords__pc');
    }

    parentElements.forEach(function(parent) {
      const child = parent.querySelector('#related-keywords');
      if (child) {
        childElement = child;
        return;
      }
    });

    if (childElement && isElementInViewport(childElement)) {
      if (!isTargetVisible) {
        dataLayer = dataLayer || [];
        dataLayer.push( {"event":"fireEvent","eventData":{"event_name":"view_content","event_parameter":{"view":0,"event_label":"view_search_result_related_keyword","event_gp1":"yohji yamamoto"},"commerce_data":null}} );
        isTargetVisible = true;
      }
    } else {
      isTargetVisible = false;
    }
  });

  function isElementInViewport(element) {
    const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
    return (
      rect.top >= 0 &&
      rect.left >= 0 &&
      rect.bottom <= window.innerHeight &&
      rect.right <= user_w_size
    );
  }
</script>

<script>
  function gaPager(pagenum) {
    dataLayer = dataLayer || []
    if (false) {
        ga('send', 'event', 'ui_action', 'search', 'click_category_page_no', {'dimension1': pagenum});

<script>
  window.addEventListener('load', function(){
    $(function(){
      // ハートのlikeボタン
      $('.like_item a').click(function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        var $a = $(this);

        var url = '/ajax/likes/create';
        if ($a.hasClass('on')) {
          url = '/ajax/likes/destroy';
        }

        $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: url,
          dataType: 'json',
          data: { item_id: $a.data('id') },
          success: function(data) {
            // Synchronize heart icon style between grid and list view.
            $(`[data-id=${$a.data('id')}]`).toggleClass('on')
          },
          error: function(xhr, textStatus, error) {
            var res = $.parseJSON(xhr.responseText);
            var message = '更新に失敗しました。';
            if (res['error_message'] !== undefined) {
              message = res['error_message'];
            }
            alert(message);
          }
        });

        return false;
      });

      // 商品詳細のlikeボタン
      $('#js-like-button').click(function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        var $a = $(this);
        var $parent = $(this).closest('.like_button_set');
        var $label = $(this).find('span');

        if ($a.hasClass('on')) {
          // unlike
          var url = '/ajax/likes/destroy';
          var labelText = $(this).data('off-label');
        } else {
          // like
          var url = '/ajax/likes/create';
          var labelText = $(this).data('on-label');
          <!-- Facebook Pixel Code -->
          fbq('track', 'AddToCart', {
            content_ids: $a.data('product_id'),
            content_type: 'product'
          });
          <!-- End Facebook Pixel Code -->
        }

        $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: url,
          dataType: 'json',
          data: { item_id: $a.data('id') },
          success: function(data) {
            $a.toggleClass('on');
            $label.text(labelText);
            if ($a.hasClass('on')) {
              $parent.addClass('on');
            } else {
              $parent.removeClass('on');
            }
          },
          error: function(xhr, textStatus, error) {
            var res = $.parseJSON(xhr.responseText);
            var message = '更新に失敗しました。';
            if (res['error_message'] != null) {
              message = res['error_message'];
            }
            alert(message);
          }
        });

        return false;
      });
    });
  });
</script>


<script>
  (function () {
    var params = location.search;
    var pathArray = location.pathname.split('/');
    if ( pathArray[3] === 'page' ) {
      setPageviewCustomOptions({ 'dimension3': decodeURI(pathArray[2]), 'dimension4': pathArray[4] });
    } else {
      if ( pathArray[1] === 'search' ) {
        setPageviewCustomOptions({ 'dimension3': decodeURI(pathArray[2]) });
      } else {
        setPageviewCustomOptions({ 'dimension3': decodeURI(pathArray[2]), 'dimension4': decodeURI(params) });
      }
    }
  }());
  window.addEventListener('load', function(){
    // 詳細検索UI出し分け
    var timer;
    var active_tab = null;
    var mobileWidth = 768;
    var $search_tab = $('.search_tab');
    var $search_btn_group = $('.search_btn');
    var $search_btn = $('.search_btn li');

    function resetTab() {
      if (active_tab) {
        return;
      }
      $search_tab.eq(0).css('display','block');
      $search_tab.eq(1).css('display','none');
      $search_btn_group.css('display','block');
      $search_btn.removeClass('active');
      $search_btn.eq(0).addClass('active');
      active_tab = 0;
    }

    function windowResize(){
      if ($(window).width() < mobileWidth) {
        resetTab();
      } else {
        $search_tab.css('display','block');
        $search_btn_group.css('display','none');
        active_tab = null;
      }
    }

    windowResize();

    $(window).resize(function() {
      if (timer !== undefined) {
        clearTimeout(timer);
      }
      timer = setTimeout(function() {
         windowResize();
      }, 200);
    });

    $search_btn.click(function() {
      var index = $search_btn.index(this);
      if (active_tab == index) {
        resetTab();
      } else {
        $search_tab.css('display','none');
        $search_tab.eq(index).css('display','block');
        $search_btn.removeClass('active');
        $(this).addClass('active');
        active_tab = index;
      }
    });
  });
</script>
